DOUBLE LIFE

by

Shonda R. Bailey

 

Dedication

I dedicate this book to my beautiful, sweet, and intelligent daughter, Bailey Baltimore. Your smile makes everything I do worth it, your courage shows Mommy there is nothing she cannot do anything, and your laughter is proof that Im doing something right! 

A special thank you to the strong woman I call Mom, Rose Bailey. Mom, you are my best friend and confidant. You bring my head out of the clouds when necessary and allow me to dream when I need to. To you, I say thank you. I can only hope to be as great a person and mother.

To my tribe of friend those near and far I say thank you for supporting me, thank you for pushing me and thank you for the prayers and positive vibes put in the universe on my behalf.

Lastly, I want to acknowledge my beautiful friend, the late Tanisha Fletcher. Her strength, fight and free spirt inspired me to do this.

To everyone about to read Double Life, from the bottom of my heart, I thank you for supporting me and I hope you enjoy this novel from cover to cover and stay tuned because theres more to come!


 

Prelude

The evening sky was filled with what seemed like a million stars sparkling and shining brightly. I was calm and filled with peace, it was simply beautiful. I sat on my deck staring up at the sky, feeling truly grateful to be on this side of the living.

 

Just a year ago life was a far cry from peaceful and calm.


 

 

Chapter 1

Luxe Salon and Spa was buzzing with business, making it the hottest salon in Arlington, Virginia, minutes from the nation's capital. Clients from all over the Washington D.C. metropolitan area flock to Luxe Salon and Spa for hair, nails, and skincare services. As stylists combed, brushed, and styled heavenly creations, the spa staff tweezed, arched, and painted to perfection, owner, Sheila Holcomb stood in the doorway of her office watching the activities.  Smiling at her thoughts as they drifted back to opening day ten years ago. The first salon was in a northern Virginia, suburban town close to Washington, DC. 

It was very small, a mere nine hundred square feet. It consisted of two styling stations and a small skincare room. Their breakroom was just large enough for a small table and two chairs.  It was located on the second floor of an old office building that housed four small office suites with one central entry causing everyone to enter through a heavy wooden door with a long plate glass window that lead one steep flight of stairs.  The small space was beautifully lined with elegant cherry hardwood floors. Large floor to ceiling windows ushered in brilliant, bright light on sunny days.  Sheila and her partners decorated with anything they could find. Everything from items from home, yard sales, thrift stores, to a few pieces found near garbage dumpsters. Each piece gave the salon its character.  Their blood, sweat and tears made this small space classy and special.  They worked very hard to grow the business. Four years later that hard work paid off enabling them to purchase the building as well as each suite, remodel, redesign and redecorate, making Luxe what it is today. 

Sheila Holcomb, Mona Ferguson, and Elise Clarkson were the first employees of the salon.  They were more like sisters. It made their partnership as necessary as the air they breathed.  The staff had no clue Mona and Elise were owners and they wanted it to remain that way.  Sheila told them constantly to let the world know they owned the place but they always gave her the same response.

"Shelia, we are not trying to deal with all that crap, you can have it! said Elise as she waved her flat iron in the air. 

"You be the owner we will be the employees. Mona agreed. 

The roar of laughter interrupted Sheilas walk down memory lane.  Stylist Carlos Dubois was entertaining the ladies in a way only he could.  Sheila could depend on his antics to keep everyone entertained.  Hed been with them for about five years.  He walked in one evening, demanded to see the owner, immediately.  Sitting at the front desk Sheila raised her head, immediately taken aback by the exquisite specimen standing before her.  Carlos stood 6 foot 4 inches tall, covered in smooth skin, like Belgian chocolate.  Dressed in a black silk suit, screamed Versace.  His hair was perfectly faded, the color of coal, not a hair out of place.  Staring back at her were eyes so dark they resembled black pearls and a smile so bright Sheila swore she could see her reflection in his teeth.

"No honey let me help you, because this salon is doomed without Ms. Carlos Dubois, honey!", he replied with pursed his lips and his hand placed on his hips.

"Doomed? How is my salon doomed without Ms. Dubois? she asked surprised by his mannerisms yet thoroughly amused.

Snapping back to the here and now, Sheila noticed Mona making her way onto the styling floor headed straight for Carlos all the while throwing daggers with her eyes.  The two women had known each other for what seemed to be a lifetime. Together they experienced ups and downs, victories and defeat, their friendship has stood the tests of life.

"What, I'm not doing anything". Carlos silently mouthed to Mona while clutching imaginary pearls around his neck as she approached.

"I can hear you all the way upstairs Carlos!  You know you need to be quiet!  You are always acting up keeping the ladies laughing! said Mona feign fake disapproval of his antics before heading to the stockroom.

Entertained and amused, Sheila watched as Mona dismissed Carlos with a wave of her hand, disappearing into the stockroom.  Sheila was pretty sure Mona was smiling all the way it was a usual occurrence, as she and Carlos were always taking shots at each other.  As Sheila scanned the styling floor, she realized they were having an extremely busy day, it was only Wednesday. The salon had two other stylists, Karla, and Summer Daniels.  Both were extremely busy.  The two of them were new to the salon, having been on the team for two years.  Sheila didnt know a lot about their lives outside the salon.  Summer Daniels, twenty-three years old, was a great hairstylist and makeup artist, she could beat a face. Summer was dependable and eager to learn the business.  Karla, in her mid-thirties, on the other hand left much to be desired.  Sheila had to admit Karla was an awesome hairstylist. Her clients always looked fabulous when they left her chair, but she could use an attitude adjustment.  Mona and Elise asked why Sheila allowed her to continue working at the salon.  The answer was easy, her clientele was enormous, her business was exceptional, she was good at what she did and her clients love her.  All of which out weighted her stinky attitude. 

The Luxe team had three more members, massage therapist and second pair of twins on the team, Mario and Marvin Jones and a nail technician, Kimberly Barnes. Marvin and Mario gave the best massages Sheila had every received. The identical twins stand six feet tall, with espresso colored skin, coal black eyes framed by eyelashes the women pay good money to have. These men bring all the ladies to Luxe Salon and Spa for weekly and monthly massage appointments. The dynamic duo loves the massage industry, having worked together for their entire careers. The two live together, travel together and are practically joined at the hip. The two had been with Luxe Salon and Spa for three years. Their professionalism and stellar massage skills made Luxe Salon and Spa a household day in the Washington Metropolitan area.

The salon also had a nail technician, Kimberly Barnes. Kimmie as she was affectionally called by her coworkers was petite, barley five feet tall with naturally black hair that hung past her shoulders and a huge personality. She was all things nails; she provided a wide range of services for the salon. Everything from a basic manicure and pedicure to intricate nail designs and sculptured nails. She used natural products and did everything by hand, no drills, or electric files. She was phenomenal at what she did and Sheila truly valued her work.  Shelia loved the business, the team she and her partners. She had built on fabulous life.

She watched as her team served their clients, laughing and enjoying what they do. While she enjoyed what she saw, she felt a twinge of pain when the memory of what she discovered earlier in the day had the potential to ruin Luxe Salon and Spa.

"Ok baby I'm ready, see you soon."  Shelia replied before hanging up the phone.

She checked her makeup and hair finding everything was in place all she needed was James. Her excitement was through the roof, she decided to sit quietly and focus on calming her nerves.

Shelia remembered sitting there in that spot for an hour afraid to move wondering what could keep James from her. She prayed nothing terrible happened to him.  Sheila sat completely still for three long hours. Just as she mustered the courage to call him, Shelia heard the doorbell ring, springing up from her chair and ran to the door. She gasped when she opened the door, she almost fainted.

Chapter 14

James stood at the door dressed in a new black suit covered in blood. Sheila gasped at the sight before her.

"James what happened, are you okay?" Shelia whispered quietly afraid to move from the spot she was standing in.

"Shelia baby she's dead, why did she do it? James asked with tears running down his face as he fell into Sheila's arms.

"What, James? What are you talking about? Who is dead, what has happened? Shelia asked him trying to hold him up. Sheila stumbled and stagger them both away from the front door and over to the sofa in the living room. James sat quietly sobbing into Sheila's neck. Sheila was so confused but she held him as he cried. After what seemed like an eternity, James began tell her what had just transpired.

"I left the house after I hung up with you. After driving about I5 minutes I realized I had forgotten your ring. I quickly turned around to head back home. I noticed my father's truck in the driveway. I walked in the house and ran upstairs to my room. Your ring was hidden in my dresser. As I walked down the hall to my room. I heard my father yell, No, Mary what have you done? I stopped at my parents bedroom door, knocking, and calling out to my father. I kept knocking and finally he opened the door, covered in blood." James told her running his hand over his head, something he did frequently when he was feeling stressed. Sheila covered he mouth afraid of what James would say next.

He stood there crying and he told me he got a call to from her job saying she hadn't come in to work. He thought her boss was crazy because he had just dropped her off at work two hours ago. My Dad hung up with my Mom's boss and tried to figure out where she could have gone." James continued telling the story more to himself as if Sheila was not in the room.

Tears filled Sheila's eyes. She really did not want to hear anymore. She was sure hearing more would tear her down to her soul but she continued to sit patiently listening.

 

"Dad said he called home and Mom answered the phone. She told him she didn't feel well so she caught the bus home. She told him she was going to lie down and that she loved him and her boys. Dad said he thought what she said was odd so he decided to work from home just in case she need him.", James told Sheila.  

"Honey, did you know your mother was at home? Did she make any noises?" Shelia asked.

"No that's just it, I was so focused on our plans I wasn't paying any attention. James replied then s suddenly became very quiet, as tears started to run down his face.

"Shelia, Mom slit her wrists! She was in my parents bathroom in the bathtub dying while I was in the next room! he cried out to her. Sheila placed both hands over her mouth, she could not believe what she had just heard. Mrs. Baker, one of her mother's best friends, had killed herself.

"I don't know, my father came home right after I left. When he went into their bedroom to see how she was feeling, she was not lying on their bed but he saw four letters. Seeing the letters, he knew something was wrong.  He walked into their bathroom and found her lying in the bathtub surrounded by blood." James told her what his father told him about, he too was crying again.

James why did she do it, did you read your letter?" Sheila asked.

"I don't know Shelia. I never even saw my letter. When they took my mothers' body out of our house in a body bag, I had to get out of there! He told her remembering vividly watching the corner rolling his mother out on a gurney.

"He knows, he and Lisa came to our house about an hour after we didn't show up at the courthouse. he told her suddenly worried about his brother.

Shelia ran to the phone to call Lisa, just the doorbell chimed. Opening the door, she saw her best friend.  Her face puffy from crying, eyes red and swollen, standing next to her was John. His tall three stature slumped over, his shoulders sagging and his eyes bloodshot but hoping his brother was there.

"He's here, come in you two, she said to them stepping aside as John rushed in to his brother.

Sheila walked behind her friends into the sitting room where James sat motionless. James and John were very close, identical twins, but more, way more than brothers. The two boys, now men were best friends. John was heading to the Air Force while James was going to study at Georgetown. They vowed to not let their personal life choices affect their relationship.  John pulled his brother to his feet, he hugged him long and hard.  Sheila and Lisa sat huddled together sobbing softly.  They had never experienced this type of pain in their lives.

The four of them sat for almost an hour saying nothing, surrounded by sadness.  Sheila heard the front door open. Sheila knew it was her mother.

Lena Montgomery, now known as Mama Lena, entered the room to find her daughter and her friends sitting there engulfed in sadness. She walked over to Shelia and Lisa, seeing their pain she hugged them tightly.  As the tears rolled down her fac she looked over at the two sons her beautiful friend had given birth to. Lena had watched these boys grow into wonderfully strong and handsome men, good men. The Bakers had done an excellent job of raising these boys. She let the girls continue to hold each other and walked over to the Baker boys.

"James, John, babies I know this is the worse pain you have ever experienced, she said through her own tears.

"Your father called me about an hour ago. He's very worried about you both, but I assured him that I knew where the two of you were. I loved your mother. She was my oldest and dearest friend and I will truly miss her. We are here for your father and you both, you understand me? she told them patting John's hands and rubbing James's head.

"Yes ma'am, finding their voices, they responded in in unison, just like when they were little Lena thought.

''Now you boys need to get home, your father is worried sick. Mama Lean told the pair, feeling extremely week herself.

James and John stood, each of them giving Mama Lena a hug, headed for the door. Following them out, Lisa and Shelia were at a loss for words. Sheila looked at the man she loved and felt helpless.  She didn't know how to make this better.  James and John adored their mother, both of their parents but Mrs. Baker was very special to them.  She didn't understand how she could take her own life and leave her sons hurting like this.  She walked towards James and fell into his arms as he leaned on his car. James held Sheila as if his life depended on their embrace. Sheila knew she needed to urge he and John to go home but she didn't want to let go. Something inside told her, their life together would change She reluctantly she pulled away, looking up into his tear stained face.

"I love you John, you know you're my big brother, she said with a smile. after walking around the car to pulling John into a tight embrace. 

John's sad face brightened a bit and a small smile appeared.

"You know it little sis, someone has to keep you in line. I love you too, he replied lovingly to his sister friend before looking over at his brother.

James, are you up for driving, man? John asked his brother softly.

"Yeah, I got it. replied James in a soft and sullen voice.

The brothers got in the car, strapped on their seat belts, and began backing out of the driveway.  Shelia and Lisa stood in front of the garage watching their friends drive away until they could no longer see them. Sheila wondering what would happen next, while Lisa stood still stunned by the death of Mrs. Baker.

"Sheila, Lisa asked her friend curiously.

"Yes, she replied.

"Why do you think she did it? Lisa asked.

"I wish I knew Lisa. I wish I knew. replied Sheila.

"She left letters I guess we will find out soon." Sheila replied to her friend.

"You girls come on in the house. I fixed dinner, lets sit down and eat, said Mama Lena.

Sheila and Lisa followed Mama Lena into the house. Sheila could tell her mother was heartbroken and sadden by Mrs. Baker's death. They had been friends for a very long time. Sheila and Lisa walked into the kitchen to see her mother had cooked smothered chicken with mushroom and onions, scalloped potatoes, and a fresh tossed salad. She even had hot buttered dinner rolls. She smiled, she knew when her mother was upset, she cooked, she always said feeding people made her feel better, helped her think things through. She was amazed at how quickly her mother could put together a meal, Sheila realized it had been quite a few hours since all of this took place, it was dinner time. After washing their hands, the three women sat down immediately joining hands to thank God for their meal.

"Lord we come before you with heavy hearts and tear stained faces first to ask that you cover our loved ones that lost a beautiful wife and mother today. While we do not understand why she chose to leave us in this way, but we pray that she accepted you in her last moments. We ask that you help us through this trying time, help her husband and sons to lean not on their own understanding but to trust in you, we also want to say thank you for the meal we are about to receive. Amen, prayed Mama Lena. Sheila and Lisa sat quietly reflecting on the words of prayer Mama Lena had just spoken.

"Sheila, I've never seen that dress before and Lisa you look very pretty too. What did you guys have planned today?" Mama Lena asked breaking the silence. Sheila stammered a bit slightly choking on her chicken.

"Nothing Mama we were just going to have a nice dinner since this was our last full week at home before leaving for school, she lied. Lisa watched the exchange but said nothing because she had stuffed food into her mouth.

"That would have been nice. I know Marilyn's unexpected death is a heavy weight on your hearts right now but you two have to be so excited about heading off to Georgetown! exclaimed Mama Lena. Sheila knew her mother was trying to lift her own spirits by talking about something exciting, her mother was hurting but she was always the person to stay strong for everyone else.

"Yes ma'am, I'm so nervous, excited but nervous, said Lisa finally finding her voice.

"Me too, Mama, do you think James is going to have to postpone starting next week or just come back home a few times this week to help with settling his Mom's affairs? Sheila asked.

"I don't know honey, give him a few days then talk to him about it, replied Lena. The ringing of the phone interrupted their conversation.

I'll get it, it's probably James saying he made it home safely.

Hello, yes sir, hi Mr. Baker, one moment. Sheila replied turning to her mother.

"Mr. Baker needs to talk to you mom, said Sheila. Sheila sat back down to eat her dinner.

"Sheila, Lisa whispered.

"What are you guys going to do, are you still getting married?

"I don't know Lisa, James was too upset, I didn't want to bring that up replied Sheila.

"I thought for sure your mother had figured it out when she said something about your dress. 

"Girl I did too, I had to think fast how to answer her!" Sheila agreed. Mama Lena walked back into the room, looking very distraught and distracted.

"What's wrong Mom? Sheila asked suddenly worried about her mother.

"Marilyn left a letter for me and Marvin wants me to come over to read it, she replied.

Why would she leave one for you? What could it say? Sheila asked worrying about her mother and now James.

"I don't know the answer to either of those questions, but I guess I'm about to find out, Mama Lena replied staring at her daughter.

 

~

Sheila sat at the table with Mona and Elise quietly reflecting on that day. She had really forgotten the two ladies were there hanging on to her every word until Mona cleared her throat.

"Sheila, Sheila, come back to us, what happened, why did James mother kill herself? Mona asked excitedly.

"Yes, what did the letter say and what happened between you and James? added Elise urging Sheila to continue her story.

"My mother and I went to Baker's house the next day. Mr. Baker gave my mother the letter addressed to her and gave her some alone time to read it.", Sheila told them going back to that day.

"Was James there? " Mona asked eagerly. Sheila was so focused on the memories she ignored the question.

"I thought my mother needed some privacy, so I headed out back to see James. He and John were in the back on the deck talking. I walked over to where he was standing and hugged him from behind.  He turned around and hugged me tight, he then looked at his brother and asked if he could give us some privacy. John agreed, but before going inside he also gave me a long tight hug.  It was all weird. It was like they were saying goodbye without actually saying it." Sheila said aloud still seeing that night clearly in her mind.

James leaned on the rail looking out over the forest green grass that covered their backyard thinking about everything that happened over the last twenty-four hours.

"Sheila, you I love you very much but I think we should break up.", James said without looking at Sheila. Sheila was stunned at what she just heard.

"What! What do you mean we should break up? Why? We love each other! Don't you love me anymore? We love each other! Sheila stammered feeling totally blindsided.

The Air Force will help me get an education, and it will send me around the world, there will be places you can't go. Georgetown is right for you Sheila, you go and make your dreams come true, he told her.

"I dont understand James. Dont you love me anymore? she said fighting to hold back tears.

"I love you Sheila but I just can't stay here, I can't live here always remembering, always reliving this. My mother was not the woman I thought she was. John and I are not who you think we are! Please honey just understand this is the best thing for us both! he told her before walked down the deck stairs, out the side gate to his car. He left without another word. Sheila stood there stunned, unable to move her feet, shocked by what had just happened.

 

Sheila and Mama Lena's drive home was very quiet. Both deep in thought, Sheila stunned by the ending of her relationship and his announcement that he was going in the Air Force and Mama Lena, shocked by the secrets Marilyn had revealed in the letter she left for her. Sheila could no longer hold back the tears. She felt her world crumbling around her. The man she loved the only man she ever loved next to her father who died when she was nine years old, had dumped her without a valid explanation. Next week she was to begin a new chapter in her life, a chapter that would lead her into adulthood and it was supposed to be with James and now that was no longer the case. How could he do this to her?

"Sheila, baby do you want to talk about it? Mam asked.

"Mama, he broke up with me, he's not going to Georgetown, he's going to the Air Force with John, she told her.

"No baby he loves you, but Marilyn kept some very important secrets from all of us and they have changed James and John's lives forever, replied Mama Lena. Lena pulled into their driveway, turned off the ignition then turned to talk to her daughter.

"Sheila honey, let's sit out on the deck tonight and talk. I have something to tell you. When I finish you will understand, it will still hurt like hell but you will understand." Sheila knew this was some heavy stuff because her mother did not usually use language like that.

It was a clear and calm August night. The two women sat quietly on the deck watching the stars twinkle brightly in the sky. Sheila wondered how long it would be before she would get the chance to sit out like this once school began next week. Even with all this going on she was still very excited about starting school. She wasn't sure of what would be her major, she knew she had to somehow factor in her love for the beauty industry. Taking cosmetology in high school was a great move. It enabled her to get her license at eighteen, which means she could work while in school. Her tuition was not an issue, her father's social security, life insurance and military pensions took care of that as well as a few academic scholarships. She was leaning toward a liberal arts degree something with art, maybe art history, or science degree maybe chemistry. A product line could be in her future. She realized she had not really thought about her dreams in a while. She was submerged in her relationship with James, their impending marriage, their life together. She had forgotten about her own dreams. Well her relationship was over so she had all the time in the world to think about her dreams, she thought sadly.

"Sheila, baby what are you thinking about? asked Mama Lena.

"My future at Georgetown, what I plan to study, how to mix it all with my love for doing hair. You know, somehow make it work. I also just realized that I have been really wrapped up in me and James lately but now that he doesn't want me in his life anymore, I have a lot of time to focus on myself, she replied.

"Sheila, James loves you very much, but honey his world has just been interrupted. His mother took her own life and left him and his brother. She kept a secret from them honey, she shared that secret with me in the letter she wrote me, she told Sheila.

"What kind of secret is so bad that would make her kill herself and leave her husband and children? asked Sheila.

"First she was diagnosed with breast cancer and she didn't tell her family. She was dealing with it alone; she did not tell anyone not even Marvin. Sheila, she lied to Marvin, about James and John. Marilyn had an affair and became pregnant with James and John by another man. That man was Marvin's brother, James, and John's Uncle Mitchell. Mitchell wanted nothing to do with the boys and he blackmailed Marilyn. He held the information over her head for the boy's entire lives until he died from AIDS complications. He constantly threatened to tell Marvin if she didn't do whatever he wanted. He made her do anything and everything from sexual favors to giving him money. Sheila honey in her letter to me, she admitted that she had been diagnosed with full blown AIDS last week. She was afraid to tell Marvin but she knew she had to tell him everything for his health and safety. She asked me to do it in the letter because she didn't have the courage to do so or to even go on. Baby that's why she killed herself, she said she did not want cancer and AIDS to slowly kill her and have her babies watch her die."

Sheila sat across from her mother listening and watching the tears roll down her face as she spoke about Mrs. Baker. It was like watching a daytime soap opera, but it was real.

"Mom does James know all of this now?" asked Shelia. "He knows about the cancer diagnosis as well as Uncle Mitchell was his real father. Until earlier today Marvin did not know about her having contracted HIV/AIDs I had to break that news to him, I could not keep that from him any longer, she told Shelia. "Mom, how did he take it? asked Sheila. Lifting her glass of red wine to her mouth and taking a long sip, she placed the glass on the table, then looked at her daughter. "Baby he knew everything; he knew about the affair and the cancer because she told him in her letter as well as her having HIV/AIDs. He didn't tell me how or when he found out about the HIV/AIDS diagnosis, but just that he knew the truth. He said he has known for a long time, but he didn't care he loved her and he realized that she probably didn't have much longer to live so he would make her last days on this earth happy. He said she endured a lifetime of pain at the hands of his evil brother to ensure her family a lifetime of happiness, Mama Lena explained. "Mom what about his health, does he have the virus too? Sheila asked. "I didn't ask him honey, I decided he needed to have some level of privacy, I did what Marilyn asked me to, that was enough, she replied. "Wow so that's what James meant when he said he and John where not who we thought they were, said Sheila. "Honey he's dealing with a lot, he's very angry at the world, his mother and maybe even himself in some ways. You must give him space to deal with this in his own way. Next week you will begin a new life and it is filled with possibilities. I love James, I've watched him grow into a wonderful man, but you are my daughter and it is my responsibility to see that you continue to grow into the beautiful woman I know you will be. I know this hurt, if you love him you will have to let him go. If you two are meant to be it will come back to you. Do you understand me honey? asked Mama Lena.

"Yes, ma'am more than you will ever know. Mona and Lisa were quietly staring at Shelia, both stunned and shocked.

Sheila snapped back to the present focusing on her friends. Smiling at the look of astonishment and sadness on their faces.

"Oh, my goodness Sheila, did you ever see him again before today? asked Mona.

"Not until my junior semester of college. He sent a letter to my mother's house and she mailed it to me. He told me how he was doing and some of the places he had visited already. He apologized for leaving the way he did asked me to forgive him for hurting me the way he did. Then he told me to keep reaching for the stars and I never heard from him again. His father had a private funeral for his mother. The only people there was my mother, myself, Lisa, Mr. Baker and John, James didn't come, Sheila told them.

"He didn't go to his mother's funeral! asked Elise.

"Sheila, I know you were devastated! exclaimed Mona.

"No, my mother has always had a way of making muddy water clear. She helped me understand that what James was dealing with had nothing to do with me. He had to deal with it in his own way. I couldn't fault him for that. Yes, it hurt and it took a long time to get him out of my system, but I guess I never really did, I just glossed over it and moved on with my life, she told her friends.

"How do you feel now especially after seeing him seemingly happy and healthy?" asked Elise.

"I'm numb to be completely honest, Sheila replied. Numb was not strong enough to describe what Sheila was really feeling. Seeing James Baker has turned her inside to mush! She loved every inch of that man and she never really stopped, he always had a piece of her heart. Sheila needed to get away from the girls to have a moment to herself. This walk down memory lane has brought some real emotions to light and she needed time to think.

"Mona, Elise I need a few days to get my head on straight. Summer and Carlos can work closely with you guys to keep everything moving smoothly, Sheila told them.

"Girl, take all the time you need, your world has been turned upside down! said Elise.

"Yes, honey take some time off, we can handle things around here with Carlos and Summer in place we can keep a closer eye on Monique! Mona said promisingly.

"Thank you, ladies, I have a lot on my plate and my head is spinning. I really appreciate and love you guys for this.

 

Chapter 15

Charles sat behind his desk reviewing a few contracts when Karl opened his office door.

"Karl, man I had the door closed for a reason. he barked without looking up from his desk.

"Charles, the police are here to see you. Karl said after clearing his throat to get Charles attention.

Police what are you talking about? Charles questioned as he lifted his head from his desk. Karl stood in front of him with two plain clothed detectives.

"Mr. Holcomb, we'd like to speak with you about an official police matter, said one detective.

"Sure, gentlemen come in. said Charles.

"Thank you, Karl, how may I help you gentlemen today? Charles said dismissing Karl and giving his attention to the detectives.

"Mr. Holcomb, my name is Detective James Baker and this is my brother and partner Detective John Baker.

"Well that is obvious youre twins. It's a pleasure to meet you gentleman. Again, how may I help you today?

"Mr. Holcomb do you know a Ms. Desiree Franklin, who resides at 22456 Fern Way, Unit I03, Alexandria VA? asked John.

"Yes, I am familiar with Ms. Franklin, what is this about?

"Well visits like this are never easy for us. Ms. Franklin was found dead in her home this morning. Her body was identified by her cousin, a Monique Morris, said James as he read from his notes.

"Dead! What do you mean dead? I just spoke with her last night around eight thirty, Charles told them.

"You spoke with her? Where were you when you spoke with her? asked James.

"I was leaving a business dinner I had with a vendor at the Saint Germaine Hotel, Charles answered.

"The Saint Germaine, that's very interesting. Mr. Holcomb, do you know a woman named Monique Morris? asked John.

"Monique Morris works for my wife, what does Monique have to do with this?

"Mr. Holcomb, Ms. Morris believes you may have something to do with her cousin's death, John said to Charles watching his reaction closely.

"What the hell are you talking about? Monique knows what kind of relationship Desiree and I had, why would she say that? She's the one that hated her cousin, she always has. She told me herself. She hated Desiree because her mother was always comparing the two of them. Constantly saying Monique should be more like Desiree. What the hell is she talking about? Charles asked, more to himself than the detectives.

"Mr. Holcomb are you sleeping with Monique? Before you answer that question Mr. Holcomb please know that Monique has told us that she has tried to break things off with you and you will not leave her alone, warned James.

"She told you what? That woman has been lying up with me willingly for years. When she found out I was seeing her cousin and Desiree was pregnant she lost her mind. She demanded that I get rid of Desiree and the baby! exclaimed Charles.

"Baby Mr. Holcomb, what baby? asked John.

"Desiree is pregnant, is the baby okay? asked Charles.

"Mr. Holcomb, Ms. Franklin was not pregnant, replied John.

"What do you mean she was not pregnant? Charles exclaimed in shock.

"No baby is what he means Mr. Holcomb. Did you? asked James.

"Did I what? replied Charles.

"Did you get rid the baby by murdering Desiree? asked John.

"Hell no, I wasn't happy about the pregnancy, I mean the fake pregnancy, but I didn't kill her! Charles said angrily.

"So, who did you have dinner with before you spoke with Desiree? asked James.

Charles thought about Desiree, the arguments with Sheila and now this. He decided it was time for him to come clean.

"There was no dinner, I was in a hotel room with Monique, we had sex and she left around eight o'clock last night, said she was going home for the night and said she would call me when she got home. I ordered room service around eight fifteen then I called Desiree and spoke with her for about two hours. My food was delivered at nine o'clock, maybe. After I ate my food, I decided I wanted a drink so I when down to the hotel bar and had a few drinks until about midnight. I went back up to my room, showered and went to bed. I woke this morning around six and came in to work, Charles explained to the detectives.

"That's a pretty elaborate as well as accurate timeline Mr. Holcomb, do you always pay such close attention to the clock? asked John.

Look Detective Baker. Charles said looking at James. "Let's not beat around the bush, you now know that I have been sleeping with two women, cousins mind you. When you have lived a secret life for this long you pay close attention to details!"

Laughing at Charles's comment James decided to take one more jab at him. "One more question Mr. Holcomb, how does your wife feel about all of this? he asked slyly.

"Detective Baker my wife has nothing to do with any of this, I am dealing with that part of my life and the well-being of my wife is none of your business, replied Charles.

James watched Charles closely. Charles's body language became agitated at the mention of Sheila. James wondered what level the agitation would arise if Charles knew that he was having dinner with his wife later tonight.

 

~

Sheila turned onto her street to see Charles's car parked in the driveway. "Damn it, she said aloud. "I don't feel like dealing with him today!" Pulling up next to his car, Sheila sat motionless except for the long deep breaths. She was hoping this would calm her nerves and restore composure. She knew she needed to deal with this thing between Charles and herself once and for all. She knew he was cheating on her and now she had proof that he was stealing from her as well. She couldn't forget the situation with Malia, she could be pregnant and she really needed to prepare herself for that. Pulling out her cell phone she checked her phone to confirm the ten oclock doctor's appointment she scheduled for Malia in the morning. Looking at her phone she noticed a new voicemail. That's odd, she thought, she didn't hear her phone ring at all. Sitting there waiting for her voicemail to play, suddenly she heard a woman's voice on the other end of the phone.

"Hello Sheila Holcomb, I've given you enough time to review the package I left in your mailbox. Interesting stuff don't you think? Your husband has been busy all over town with a lot of women and he's stealing from you. What do you think of that? Don't fret, his day is coming, he will pay the price for hurting all of us trust me. Oh, Sheila don't be surprised if you receive more shocking information about Charles soon. I will be calling you again soon, the voice said before disconnecting the call.

Sheila was angry all over again. She'd had enough of Charles and his secret life; she was done trying to figure out what to do. Opening the SUV door Sheila stepped out of the car slamming the door. She opened the front door and walked into the kitchen to find Charles sitting at the dining room table.

"Charles what are you doing here? she asked him.

"I need to talk to you Sheila, replied Charles.

"Charles I just got home from the bank, you want to come clean about stealing from my business and tell me why people are leaving messages on my cell phone about you? said Sheila.

Running his hands over clean shaven head, Charles exhaled the breath he had been holding since he heard Sheila putting her key in the front door.

"Sheila, no more lies, yes I know Desire Franklin and yes I've been having an affair with her, Charles said taking a long pause before continuing.

"Sheila, they found her dead in her condo this morning. I'm in trouble, the police think I had something to do with it! Sheila sank down in the dining chair across from Charles.

"What, Charles that girl is dead! Charles the baby is gone too? asked Sheila.

"No, it was all a lie, she wasn't pregnant, but she is dead. Someone suffocated her. The police came to my office earlier today asking questions, said Charles.

"Charles you have been doing some foul stuff lately but I don't think you are a killer! said Sheila.

"Sheila I'm going to tell you everything, I can't carry all of this around anymore. As you suspected, I mean you know I've been, I mean I was sleeping with Desiree for about two years, he stammered. "I moved her here because the traveling back and forth to Chicago was getting to be too much. I never had any intention of marrying her or leaving you and Malia, he told her.

"Charles did Corey know about this? she asked him shocked that he finally told her the truth.

"No Sheila no one knew until she moved here last week. I found out she and Monique, your receptionist, are cousins, he continued.

"I already knew that Charles I told you remember. You lied and said you didn't know they were related! said Sheila.

"Sheila honey please let me tell you everything. I found out Monique was Desiree's cousin a few weeks ago when I dropped by Desiree's condo, she opened the door, he told her.

"Yes, and you continued to lie about knowing they were related! Sheila said ignoring Charles request that she be quiet and let him talk.

"Sheila. Charles said hesitantly. "Spit it out Charles, snapped Sheila growing tired of this conversation.

"I've been sleeping with Monique also! Yes, I knew she was stealing from you and I did use money from the Luxe account to keep both women, he told her bracing for the eruption of anger he saw rising in her face.

Sheila stared at Charles as if she had never seen him before. Sheila opened her mouth to speak but nothing came out, she attempted to speak again but again nothing.

"Sheila baby I'm sorry, I can't explain why I did these things but I did, I slept with both of those women and actually a few more but the only one claimed to pregnant was Desiree. That DVD and recording sent to you was a lie I swear it was! he pleaded.

"You were sleeping with that evil ass Monique Charles! You allowed me to walk around being made a fool of at the hands of Monique Morris! Charles you recommended I hire her! Were you sleeping with her then? she asked him.

"Yes. Charles replied looking directly into Sheilas eyes.

"I can't believe you did this to me, to us! said Sheila yelled.

"Sheila baby, I need your support now. I did not kill Desiree, I believe it was Monique, she's trying to frame me because I told her it was over between us! he pleaded with Sheila.

"Charles, do you really think I will lift a finger to help you after all that you've done to me? asked Sheila, her voiced laced with sarcasm.

"Sheila, baby please I need your help! I didn't kill that girl, I swear! Charles pleaded to Sheila.

Sheila stared at Charles her face expressing pure disbelief and disgust that Charles expected her to help him or even believe him after all that he had done.

It had to be Monique, she said she has hated Desiree all of her life, she told me to get rid of Desiree and the baby or she would make sure you knew about all of this. I know she's the one that sent that package and left you the message just now. She said she didn't, it was someone else but I know it was her!" Charles continued.

Sheila sat at the table stunned at what Charles had revealed. She had her suspicions about Charles's infidelity and even stealing from her business but she was totally blown away by all of this. Murder, could Charles really have murdered this woman? Is he trying to blame someone else now, covering it up, she asked herself? Sheila sat quietly processing all that Charles had just told her. She felt her phone vibrating that would explain why she did not hear her phone ring earlier. Looking down at the phone she saw a phone number she did not recognize. Thinking it may be another anonymous call she sent it to voicemail. She placed the phone on the table and looked at Charles.

"Charles, please leave. I am tired of dealing with this and I just can't right now. You made this bed and you will have to lie in it. I can't help you. You have been lying to me, you have cheated on me and now you have the audacity to want, no excuse me, beg and plead for my help. Sheila summarized still in total disbelief that husband would do all of this.

Sheila, I am telling you the truth, no more lies, not more cover up this is the truth. Charles told her.

Charles, if Desiree had not been killed you would still be lying and cheating. I can't help you and I want a divorce! There's no coming back from this! Pack bag and get out please! Sheila yelled out.

Both Sheila and Charles stood shocked by her words. She wasnt sure if she really wanted a divorce at all but she was tired of Charles and all of this.

Charles please just leave for tonight., Sheila asked quietly.

Charles stood there with his head hanging down. He thought if he came clean, she would at least help him even if their marriage was over, but he realized his betrayal, lying and cheating was something Sheila could never forgive. He stood there watching as Sheila walked out of the kitchen and what felt like out of his life forever.

Sheila walked up the stairs towards her bedroom. She stopped and knocked on Malia's door, it was time for her to tell Malia what was going on. Knocking and softly opening Malia's door she saw her daughter was sitting on her bed writing in her journal. Until now she wasn't sure if Malia kept a journal.

"Hey Liaboo, what you doing, sweetie? asked Sheila.

Mom, Im scared. Malia said in a soft, low voice as she leaned her head on her mothers shoulder. Sheila pulled her daughter close. It had been a long time since she held the daughter.

I know you are honey but you have to relax and wait until we see the doctor. Sheila said as she stroked her daughters hair.

Malia, you have an appointment at ten in the morning, once we know for sure we will decide what to do. Did you eat today? Sheila asked her daughter. If Malia was pregnant, she needed to begin taking care of herself Sheila thought to herself.

"Yes, ma'am I did, I'm not really hungry right now though, Malia replied.

"Okay I'm going to take a bath, Sheila told her daughter as she closed her bedroom door.

As Sheila walked down the hall towards her bedroom, she realized that her daughter had matured in the past few weeks.

She found Charles standing at his dresser removing clothing and placing them into his suitcase. He stopped packing and watched his wife walk past him into their bathroom. Hed hoped Sheila would have calmed down enough to want to talk to him, but she walked by him without a word.

Sheila stepped into the bathroom, turned on the water. She watched the hot water puddle on the floor of the tub, steaming hot and swirling around. She poured in a few capfuls of vanilla and sugar scented bubble bath as Charles entered the bathroom. She hoped would not try to talk to her about leaving again. She had nothing more to say about it tonight. Thankfully he said nothing, he just grabbed his toiletries and left the room.

Sheila thought of James as she watched the tub fill with fluffy white suds. She remembered he was planning to text her with dinner detail. She went to retrieve her cell phone from her purse. She noticed Charles had finished packing his suitcase with clothing and begun filling his travel tote with cologne and other toiletries from the bathroom. She could tell he was packing slower than necessary but she did not care she just wanted him to leave so she could enjoy her bath. Charles finally finished his extended packing tasks then began gathering his things to leave, but attempted to plead his case one last time.

"Sheila baby please, I know I've hurt you but we can work this out." Charles begged once more.

"Charles, at this point there is nothing to work out, you broke your vows, not once, not twice but at least three times with three different women and those are the ones I know about. You have been lying for months. You have been stealing from me and giving my money to your women. What makes you think I could forgive you for that and not to mention forgive you tonight? she said to him.

"Sheila please you and Malia should not be here in the house alone. At least let me stay in the guest room. Charles begged.

"No Charles. She interrupted him holding up her hand. "Please take a moment to speak with your daughter on your way out, by the way she has a doctor's appointment in the morning at ten, we will know then if she is pregnant or not. Good night, she said to him before walking into the bathroom and closing the door behind her.

"What friends Sheila, who are you going out with? he asked her through the door. Suddenly the bathroom door flew open! Sheila faced Charles her eyes blazing with fire!

"You have the audacity to question what I'm doing and with whom when you have an undisclosed number of mistresses, one woman is now dead and as well as her unborn child? Charles Holcomb, get the hell out of my face and this house!" She then turned and walked into her bathroom slamming the door behind her!

Charles walked out of their bedroom softly closing the door and walked down the hall. He stopped at Malia's door, knocking softly when he didn't hear her respond, he slowly opened her door, to find her sleeping quietly on her bed. He walked in and kissed her forehead whispered "I'm sorry Liaboo and I love you". He turned and walked out of the room closing the door behind him. Malia opened her eyes letting the tears she held in, fall from her eyes.

Sheila pulled her SUV around to the hotel valet. Now that she was here, minutes from being alone with James Baker again, she wasn't so sure it was a good idea. Sheila loved James with every bone in her body, at one time. Seeing him again has been more than a shock. She couldn't forget the reason why she was seeing him again. He was here to investigate her husband, how ironic.

Sheila smoothed the wrinkles from her dress then patted her hair, before headed into the Omni Hotel. She and James were planning to meet in the bar for drinks and then have dinner in the hotel restaurant.

The hotel was beautifully decorated with rich hues of nature. Olive and burgundy seating accented with gold carpets and fixtures giving an expensive feel to the atmosphere. Sheila, flustered by his intense stare, suddenly realized her feelings had not changed, she still loved him. The voice of reason to her to turn and leave but her feet were anchored in place. Sheila felt a tap on her shoulder, she turned to find John Baker, standing behind her arms open wide ready wrap her in a bear hug just like when they were teenagers.

It felt like old times to Sheila, for just moment she could forget about her lifes issues and have fun.

Charles watched his brother try to squeeze the life out Sheila with a hug. It made him feel good. Sheila was still the love of his life, even after his whole world had been turned upside down. The decision to end his relationship with Sheila was a hard one to make. He was really messed up by his mother's suicide and all the secrets she revealed. Rolling their eyes and laughing at James and his appetite, the two headed to the restaurant leaving James standing alone.

Three hours later Sheila, James and John sat sipping coffee and nibbling on desserts.

Sheila listened quietly, slightly surprised to hear that James never married. She had to admit to herself that she wondered over the years how he was doing, whether he had a wife and kids, she now had her answer.

James continued.

The young and fresh out of high school girl you once knew is still here, but the mature and responsible woman I have become needs to close one door before opening another. "James, I understand but please give me space and time to handle this, she replied unable to break eye contact with James. She knew he was serious

"I can and will do that for you Sheila, He assured her.

"Well. Sheila said reluctantly breaking their stare taking that moment compose herself.

"Dinner was great, it was so good to see John. You two are still as close as ever, she told him.

"Yes, we have grown as close as twin brothers, could be, he laughed.

"You think? said Sheila mused.

"We both dealt with Mom's death and secrets in different ways. John's life changed when he met his wife and they had the kids. He said he realized that Mom kept those secrets for all those years for us when he looked into the eyes of his children and he knew he would walk through fire for them. Me, on the other hand, well I decided to work and drink myself to death and run from it all. That worked for a while until one day about a year ago I found myself sitting in a dark room, with a half empty bottle of liquor and my service revolver, said James.

Astonished by what James had just revealed, Sheila sat with her hand covering her mouth and eyes widened. "Jamie, no! she said through her fingers.

"My cell phone rang and I looked down to see my nephew calling, John's oldest son James, named after me of course. That young man means the world to me. I answered, planning to hear his voice for the last time, James said remembering that conversation.

"Hello. James said into the receiver.

"Georgetown, really man that's big! You know I had a full scholarship to go there too, son, James told my nephew feeling genuinely happy to hear his news.

James sat silently, tears streaming down his face. just then I understood what my brother felt for his son. At that very moment I knew it was time to forgive our mother for taking her life and leaving me. Sheila was speechless, tears running down her face, her heart and mind filled with emotions. She was so moved by hearing that James thought of suicide. So many emotions filled her heart at that moment. She was saddened to know that James carried such pain and hatred for so long but also elated to know he found his way out. My mother spoke with your father, I mean Mr. Marvin quite often, especially when his health started to deteriorate. She would go over every day to help the nurse with getting his dinner. She said she knew your mother would want someone he knew around." Sheila continued remembering how Mr. Marvin smiled whenever she came over to visit James and John.

Once I let go of the anger and pain, I realized the courage and love it took for my father, Marvin, to ignore the truth and keep that secret. Sheila sat listening to James feeling all his pain. Hearing about his life after their breakup even after all these years jarred her emotions. James spoke to her with an honest, open, and genuine truthfulness. He didn't hide his expressions. He spoke as if he had forgotten she was there. So many feelings began to flood Sheila's mind and heart. She wanted to wrap her arms around him and tell him everything would be okay but she knew that was not an appropriate action at this time.

She knew it was time to bring this night to an end before she let her heart overrule her mind. "Jamie this has been a wonderful evening; dinner was great and the walk down memory lane was just what I needed. I have to call I it a night, I have a busy day tomorrow planned for tomorrow, said Sheila. "Yes, beautiful lady it has been and I hope I haven't offended you with my openness about my feeling for you. I may never get this chance again, he told her.

As I told you before my life has been turned upside down with Charles antics, issues with my daughter and life as I know it. So, I must ask you to give me some time to process and deal with all of that has fallen into my lap. she said to him, sincerely.

Taking Sheila's hands into his, James looked deeply into Sheila's eyes and said, "Sheila Montgomery Holcomb, the love I have for you will not allow me to do anything that would hurt you. I'm not here to tear down your world any more than life has done already. I'm here to rebuild it. So yes, I will give you all the space and time you need. Whatever choices you make I will accept. Thank you for dinner tonight and please promise me that we will never lose contact again."

"I promise Mr. James "Jamie" Baker, I promise I will not lose contact with you ever again no matter what direction my life takes." Sheila meant every word, even if her mind was telling her, life as she knew it was becoming more chaotic by the minute.

 

Chapter 16

Sheila drove home in silence. The bright lights of downtown gave her SUV a strobe light effect. Her mind was racing as she replayed the conversations, she and James had over dinner tonight. She kept hearing his words repeatedly. The words that if he ever had the chance, hed take her back and never let her go. Charles was the only other man she'd ever loved as much as James. Chuckling to herself at the thought that just passed through her mind, she didn't like Charles very much now, but she knew she still loved him. Her relationship with Charles was over, she was sure of that and seeing James, having dinner with him and John, walking down memory lane felt good but she had to be honest she still loved Charles and love doesn't go away overnight.

The time with James felt good, good, almost too good she thought to herself. Hearing James tell her that he'd never stopped loving her and he would stop at nothing to get her and Malia in his life was still weighing heavily on her heart. She realized tonight she still loved James, but she couldn't ignore what she and Charles had. Their relationship has been destroyed but she did love her husband and their family. She was no longer sure if she was in love with Charles but she couldn't deny the love she did have for him. Sheila knew she had to put distance between herself and James. She had to close Charles door before she could open the one marked James.

Sheila needed to talk with two very important people, God himself and her pastor, the Reverend Jeremiah Buchman. Only God himself could help her with this. Sheila pulled into the driveway. She turned off the ignition and exhaled a long deep breath. She leaned over to grab her purse when she noticed the light blinking on her cell phone. She'd missed a call. That was odd her phone never rang. She pressed play to listen to the voicemail.

"Hello Sheila, looks like your husband has gotten himself into some trouble, the voiced filled with amusement. "The hot little mistress and the love child are dead and Mr. Charles Holcomb is running scared as he should be. His lying and cheating have caught up to him. I guess by now you know about his affair with Monique. He told you before I could, one point for him. Tell your husband he can't use people until he's done with them and then throw them out like trash. He will pay for all that he has done, I promise you that! yelled the voice before the voicemail ended. Sheila sat holding the phone absolutely shocked by what she heard. Charles has gotten himself into a very dangerous situation. He is suspected of murder of that woman and her child, he has been stealing from my business and cheating with one of my employees, now there's someone out to destroy him.

Sheila went into the house immediately and up the stairs to check on Malia. She opened the door just enough to poke her head in. She saw Malia sleeping soundly she heard her soft breathing and instantly felt relieved. She quietly closed her daughter's bedroom door and walked down the hall to her bedroom. She took off her coat and threw it across the chaise lounge and headed to the bathroom where she stripped down to nothing and pulled on her soft and fluffy robe.

She decided to call Charles he needed to know about this latest voicemail message. Sheila grabbed the cordless phone and dialed Charles's cellular number.

After four rings she heard a groggy Charles on the other end, "Sheila baby what's wrong are you and Malia okay?" Sheila could hear urgency mixed with sleepiness in his voice. A vision of Charles lying in the bed shirtless in silk pajama pants flashed into her mind. She could even smell his aftershave. A wave of nostalgia flowed through Sheila, before the sound of Charles calling her name broke her trance.

"Sheila baby are you okay?" he asked again now fully awake.

"Yes, Charles I'm here, Malia and I are fine. I'm sorry I didn't mean to scare you by calling this late, she replied calmly.

"No, its okay, he said assured her.

"Charles, I got another voice mail message on my cellular phone again. This time the person knew everything, Desiree and the baby being dead, your affair with Monique and the fact that the police suspect you, she told him.

"What! Sheila was it a man or woman? he asked.

"The voice was distorted so I couldn't make out whether it was a man or woman, she told him.

Releasing a long sigh before saying, "Sheila, Monique has to be responsible for all this!" "Charles, I know Monique and her attitude leave nothing to be desire, wait you have been sleeping with her so I guess you found something, but do you really think she's capable of murdering her own cousin and her child even though Desiree was not really pregnant? Sheila said to Charles.
