"Calvin, I mean Karl what is wrong with you, I'm married to your business partner!"

"Yes, my business partner, Charles Holcomb. The scumbag you call a husband is on his way to jail! I can't believe it took me this long to finally get him out of your life. I sent letters, messages, picture after picture and DVDs."

"You sent that stuff? What do you mean he's going to jail! yelled Sheila.

Yes, I had to make you see what kind of man Charles really is. He being booked as we speak! he told Sheila as he handed her a glass of champagne.

"What are you talking about, Charles didn't kill Desiree and she wasn't pregnant! The police already know she wasn't pregnant. I don't want any champagne! We have nothing to celebrate! Why are you doing this Karl! yelled Shelia refusing to take the champagne filled glass from Karl's hand.

Enraged by her rejection, Karl grabbed Sheila around the neck and slammed her against the wall. "Dammit Sheila, for years I have watched that man treat you terribly! I've done everything but tell you to your face what he has been doing! I've shown you nothing but love, tenderness, and care and this is how you treat me and the love I have for you? All I ask is that you have a glass of champagne with me to celebrate your freedom but all you can do is talk about Charles! He's done, I made sure of that! Now take the damn glass and sit down! he yelled pushing Sheila down into the chair.

Terrified, Sheila realized no one knew she was in trouble and she didn't have any way of getting help.

"Calvin what did you do? Sheila asked quietly.

"My name is Karlton McKenzie! Stop calling me Calvin! I need to make you see how much I love you! he yelled pulling a gun out of his waistband he then began tapped the gun against his head.

Sheila tried to remain calm, she had to find out what was going on in Karl's head. "I'm sorry Karl, I didn't mean to upset you. May I ask you a question? she said softly.

"What? Karl replied.

You and I had a quite a few freshman classes together, we studied together all the time throughout our college years, right? she asked him. Grabbing the photograph of them as college freshman, Karl dropped it in Sheila's lap.

"Look at that fat, sloppy kid. I was hideously ugly, had bad teeth and a complete nerd. You, Lisa, your friends, all of you were beautiful and out of my league! You and Lisa were the only people that were ever truly nice to me. You wanted nothing from me but friendship, no tutoring sessions, no, write my paper requests, nothing but real friendship, he quietly told her.

"Karl none of us looked at you as a fat sloppy kid! We thought you were a smart guy that was going places, you were our friend. What puzzles me is your love for me! You and Lisa studied together more often than I because you had the same major. You spent way more time with her than me. Why me? she asked genuinely wanting to know the answer.

"Lisa was more like the sister I never had but you, Sheila you had this natural glow. A light that brightened every room you entered. You treated everyone the same. You made people smile and be happy. You made me believe I could be anything I wanted to be, until I looked in the mirror and saw my reflection. I vowed to change how I looked, make myself better, more handsome, and attractive so I could tell you how I felt one day. I kept in touch with Lisa but only through emails.

She never knew you were here living as Karl and not Calvin? Sheila asked.

No, I told her I lived in Europe, she never mentioned me to you? he asked.

Well she would say from time to time that she received emails from many of our friends including yourself but that was it.

Sheila you deserve so much better than Charles. I love you and Malia, he told her.

Karl you said you made sure Charles was going to be out of my life forever what did you do? she asked.

I killed Desiree and framed Charles for it! he told her.

How can that be, the police questioned Charles already, she told him.

Charles confessed today to murdering her, the police came here and arrested him. He will never tell the police anything different if he knows what's best for him, that is, said Karl.

Karl, what did you do to make Charles confess, please tell me! she begged.

Shut up Sheila! Why do you still care about him after all he's done, yelled Karl.

Karl, Charles is my husband and Malia's father, that's why I still care! she told him. Karl crossed the room in three steps stopping directly in front of Sheila, pressing the gun barrel firmly between her eyes.

"You don't love me! You don't appreciate what I've done here! All of this for you! I should kill Malia anyway, no both of you and let Charles rot in jail! he yelled.

No, no please don't hurt my daughter, she pleaded with Karl. At that precise moment the cordless phone rang.

"I'm sure that is Lisa, I have her car. I drove it here, cried Sheila.

"Answer it and tell her to come here you need her help and tell her to bring Malia! yelled Karl.

"No please Karl don't hurt them, I will do whatever you want just don't hurt either of them, Sheila begged.

"Whatever I want? said Karl.

"Yes, whatever you want! replied Sheila.

"Answer the phone and tell her everything is fine you will be back soon and don't try anything or its goodbye Lisa and Malia. You got that! he yelled.

"Yes anything, just don't hurt them, Sheila replied.

~

At the police station, Charles sat in the interrogation room waiting and wondering what Karl was doing. He was worried sick; he would kill Karl if he put his hands-on Sheila or Malia. Detective Jackson and James stood outside watching Charles.

What do you think man? Detective Jackson asked.

Something is not right about this and I cant put my finger on it, James replied

Im going in to see what I can find out, he said opening the interrogation room.

"Mr. Holcomb, lets discuss this confession, shall we, Detective Jackson asked.

There's nothing to discuss, I killed her because she was pregnant and I didn't want the kid. She said she wasn't going to get an abortion, so I killed her, Charles said clearly irritated es.

James listened wondering why Charles was blatantly lying. He knew she wasn't pregnant because he was told when we searched his office. He swore that he had nothing to do with her murder, why is he lying.

"It doesn't matter if she was pregnant or not, when she told me, I didn't want a kid with her, so I killed her. I'm telling you now because I cant lie to my family anymore. I have hurt them enough, it is for my familys sake, Charles told the detective.

For your family's sake? What does that mean? asked Detective Jackson.

It means I have put my family through enough with all the cheating and lies Detective, replied Charles.

James suddenly knew what Charles was doing. He needed to get to the bottom of this now! He walked into the interrogation room.

Charles do you know a Mr. Calvin Hobbes? James asked as he walked into the room.

Calvin Hobbes, no I don't know anyone by that name. Who is he? Charles replied looking at James and wonder what he was doing there.

Charles tell us about your business partner, Karlton McKenzie? said Detective Jackson.

Karl and I have known each other for a long time. I met him on the golf course about ten years ago. He has a great business mind, replied Charles clearly agitated.

Where's he from, does he have any family? asked James.

He said he's from Detroit, has no real family that I know of, replied Charles. It was obvious to both detectives the discussion was causing a great deal of stress for Charles.

Are you guys going to book me and get this over with I need to call my wife, said Charles.

Charles, we did some digging into Karl's background, came up with nothing attached to that name. Everything you know about Karlton McKenzie is a lie. His birthday, his name, his history, all lies. The one thing about Karl that did ring true was his email account," James told Charles.

You see, Karlton McKenzie's real name is Calvin Hobbes. He's a graduate of Georgetown University. He was a part of the same graduating class as Sheila and Lisa. We found that he was in contact with Lisa through emails. We investigated those emails and found they were sent from a chobbmail.com address, signed by Karlton McKenzie.

Many of their conversations where about yourself, Monique and Sheila, said Detective Jackson. We found the email address chobbesmail.com belonged to Karlton McKenzie but how could that be when Karlton McKenzie does not exist.

After further investigation we learned the email address belonged to Calvin Hobbes, said James. "We believe he killed Desiree and now Sheila and Lisa may be in grave danger. So, booking you for the murder of Desiree Franklin is out of the question, but we need you to tell us everything you know about Karlton McKenzie and why you are confessing to a crime you did not commit! James said firmly.

"Damn man why didn't you tell me all of this an hour ago! My wife and daughter are in danger! Karl, Calvin whoever he is admitted everything to me. He said he's in love with Sheila and he was tired of my disrespecting her. He threatened to kill my daughter if I didn't confess to Desiree's murder. He said he and Desiree were sleeping together, he told her to tell me she was pregnant because he wanted to break up my marriage. He said if I didn't take the fall, he would kill my daughter. That's why I called and confessed, Charles responded.

"Charles where is Sheila now!" asked James.

"She and Malia are at Lisa's house. Corey is here! he replied.

"Jackson get Corey now! said James.

"On it said Detective Jackson running out to get Corey. The two men came back into the room.

"Charles what the hell is going on? asked Corey.

"We'll explain later, get your wife on the phone now! Charles ordered. Corey pulled out his cell phone to call Lisa and handed the phone to James.

"Hey Baby! answered Lisa.

"Lisa, this is James Baker, is Sheila with you? he asked.

"Hi James, what are you doing calling me? No, Sheila went to her house to help Charles and Karl with a printer issue, I was about to call her. Is something wrong? asked Lisa becoming worried.

"Is Malia with you? James asked.

"Yes, James what's going on! yelled Lisa.

"Lisa do you remember a guy from you and Sheila's undergrad class at Georgetown named Calvin Hobbes?"

"Yes, we were all friends, I get emails from him from time to time he lives in Europe somewhere. He was quiet, he didn't have a lot of friends I think Sheila and I were the only people he talked to and that wasn't that often, we only studied together. He seemed like a nice guy. James how do you know Calvin?"

"Lisa, he changed his name to Karlton McKenzie, altered his appearance and he's been living here pretending to be someone else! He's obsessed with Sheila! He believes he's in love with her. Sheila is in great danger. He killed Desiree and forced Charles to take the fall. He also threatened to kill Malia if Charles didn't.

James! yelled Lisa. Sheila is at her house right now; you have to help her.

We are headed there now, you get Malia and come to the police station to be with your husband, now Lisa! said James.

Okay, may I speak with my husband please? asked Lisa.

James gave the phone back to Corey and turned to Charles. Man, if you love your wife as much as you say, we need to get to your house quickly! Hobbes is one sick puppy, Sheila and Malia are in danger, we don't have time to waste!"

Let's go! replied Charles.

 

Chapter 22

Karl stood very close to Sheila as she grabbed the cordless phone to answer it. Sheila prayed Lisa would be able to read between the lines and know something was wrong. Sheila pressed the button to answer the call but all she heard was the dial tone. She missed the call. Sheila needed to buy some time so she pretended to take the call.

"Hello, she said into the receiver.

Yes, Lisa I'm still here, this printer is working again, and I just stuck around to help get this proposal out the door. Oh, you're around the corner? she said looking at Karl. I think we have things under control now, but? said Sheila. "No, really you don't have to.

Sheila continued pretending to speak with Lisa. "Okay see you in a few, Sheila said before hanging up the phone.

"Why didn't you talk her out of coming? Damn, we need to get out of here, yelled Karl.

Karl wait, if we leave before Lisa gets here that's going to cause her to worry. You want everything to look normal, dont you? Sheila ask Karl. Sheila noticed Karls facial expression change.

Karl looked at Sheila suspiciously, then pointed the gun at her. He had to figure out what to do. Things were not going as planned, Sheila was supposed to be in his arms now ready to get Malia and leave, but no she was still here worrying about Charles.

Karl, Calvin, please put the gun down. You don't have to do this. I know you love me and Lisa, we were once good friends, but we grew up and changed with life. You can find love in someone else, Sheila said softly.

Just then there was a knock on the front door. Karl went to the door to see the Detective that presented the search warrant standing at the door.

Mr. Hobbes, I am Detective James Baker, I would like to come in to speak with you for a moment. Can I do that? I am not armed, is that okay? James yelled through the front door.

No, my name is not Hobbes! Its McKenzie, Karlton McKenzie and I will only talk to Sheila or Lisa! Karl yelled back.

Mr. Hobbes, I mean Mr. McKenzie, I don't think that will be a good idea. I believe you and I can sit down and have a great conversation if you just let me, replied James.

Can you hear detective? I will talk to Sheila or Lisa only. Sheila is here, get Lisa and I'll talk! Karl yelled back.

I want you Sheila. I want my friend Lisa back too. I want it to go back to the way it used to be. I did all of this for you, please Sheila, tell them you love me and you want to leave with me. Tell them! cried Karl.

Calvin I'm here, it's me Lisa, I'm coming in okay stay calm and don't hurt anyone or yourself, Lisa said.

Hell, no Lisa, you are not going in there, its too dangerous! yelled Corey.

He's right Mrs. Martin it too dangerous, we cannot let you go in there! said Detective Jackson.

Look you two, Calvin was our friend maybe I can get through to him, Lisa said softly.

"Lisa you are the only wife I have and want I need you! said Corey.

"Honey please let me do this I have to help Sheila, Lisa replied.

"I can't let you do that, all of this is my fault, it's bad enough Sheila is in there, we can't risk sending you in there too, said Charles.

"Charles this is not your fault; you had no clue just like the rest of us. You made mistakes just like the rest of us no one is perfect. Sheila and I have been through a lot of storms and this one is no different. I'm going in! Lisa told them.

"Aunt Lisa, please bring my Mom out of there safely, cried Malia.

Lisa grabbed her goddaughter and hugged her tight. "Don't worry honey, your mother and I will be fine. Sheila is not leaving you anytime soon. Never forget that, Lisa told her.

"Send Charles in here with Lisa now, right now! yelled Karl.

Lisa looked at Charles. "I'll go first, it's me he most angry with, Charles said as he and Lisa walked through the front door of, he and Sheila's home. "We're coming in Karl, please stay calm! yelled Charles.

"So, you told them everything! I should shoot you dead right now, yelled Karl. "No Karl I did what you told me to do, I confessed. The detectives figured it out on their own. I kept the story intact, said Charles.

"Where's Lisa? yelled Karl.

'Im here Calvin, I mean Karl! said Lisa walking around the corner slowly.

"Calvin I can't believe it's you, trying to make small talk hoping it would keep Karl relaxed.

"Yes, I've been here all along and the people I thought were my friends didn't even remember me! exclaimed Karl.

"Calvin you can't blame us for that when you changed everything about your appearance, and your name! How could we know it was you? said Lisa.

"Look at me Lisa, have my eyes changed? No, real friends know that eyes are the window to a person's soul. You two never really looked in my eyes! You were never really my friends, Karl said to Lisa and Sheila while waving the gun at them.

"Okay Karl please be careful we don't want that thing going off accidentally, urged Charles.

"You shut up! All of this is your fault! All the lying, all the cheating! You deserve to die for what you've done to this to this woman, yelled Karl as he grabbed Sheila. "Maybe I will just shoot her, then neither of us will have her! said Karl pressing the gun to Sheila's temple.

"No, please Calvin, don't hurt her, please! Think about Malia, if you love Sheila as much as you say then you love her daughter. She needs her mother! begged Lisa.

"Stop calling me Calvin, my name is Karlton McKenzie! he yelled pushing Sheila to the floor and placing his hands on his head. Charles realized Karl was losing control. He had to get that gun away from Karl. Charles jumped at Karl grabbing for the gun, instead he knocked them both to the ground causing the gun to fly from Karls hand and firing when it hit the floor sliding toward Lisa. Sheila ran over to Lisa.

Charles and Karl continued to fight. Obtaining the upper hand, Karl punched Charles grabbed the gun, scrambled to his feet, turned, and shot Charles hitting him in the chest. Sheila cried out loudly snapping Karl out of his trance. Karl turned around at the sound of Sheila's cry to find Sheila sitting on the floor holding Lisa as blood flowed from her body.

"Oh my God what have I done? Sheila I'm so sorry, I never wanted to hurt my friend. I'm so sorry!" "Karl please put the gun down and get help, Lisa and Charles could die! yelled Sheila. Karl stood frozen, holding the gun at his side.

"Sheila I cannot live this way anymore. I don't deserve you, I'm sorry, please forgive me. God please forgive me, Karl said as he raised the gun to his head and pulled the trigger.

Karl no! Sheila screamed as Karl's body fell to the floor.

James, Detective Jackson, and Corey heard the shots. "Go, go, go!" yelled Detective Jackson to the officers lying in wait to enter the house.

Detective Jackson exited the house,

"Baker it's clear but it's bad in there! Get the paramedics in now! he yelled to James.

"Corey, Malia wait here we will call you in we have everything secure, said James.

"No, my wife and her parents are in there man! yelled Corey as he brushed past James, pulling Malia along with him to enter the house.

"Lisa, baby are you okay? yelled Corey.

Charles lay in the corner bleeding, Karl lay dead on the floor and Sheila sat covered in blood from Lisas bleeding wound, Corey ran over to Sheila, grabbed his wife's limp body.

Lisa, baby talk to me! he cried out.

Get the paramedics, my wife has been shot! Sheila what happened? yelled Corey.

They are here, move back so they can get her to the hospital! said James. Mom are you okay? cried Malia. Yes, honey I am but Karl shot your father honey then he killed himself! Sheila told Malia.

No mommy, where is Daddy? Malia asked holding her mother tightly. The paramedics are working on him, we have to stay calm honey, Sheila told her daughter as she sobbed on her shoulder. Sheila looked around her home. She could not believe what unfolded here today.

The paramedics put Lisa in the ambulance with Corey by her side to take her to the hospital. Sheila and Malia watched as the paramedics worked feverously to stop the blood flowing from Charles's wound.

Let's go! Get him to the hospital stat! the paramedic called out as a second ambulance pulled away in route to the hospital. Sheila, I will take you and Malia to the hospital now, said James.

Thank you, Jamie. Come on honey, said Shelia holding her daughter as they turned to walk out of the kitchen.

Sheila looked back to see an officer covering Karl's body. She knew Karl did not mean to hurt any of them. Not understanding any of this, Sheila said a silent prayer for Calvin's soul. "Lord, please forgive him for he knows not what he has done. He just wanted to be loved, just like all your children. Please find a way to forgive him for the things he has done, I have. Amen, she said softly to herself.

 

 

 

 

 

~

 

Sheila, Elise, and Mona decided it was best to close Luxe Salon and Spa on the day of the funeral. Many of their clients planned to attend to show their respect for Lisa and Charles.

Sheila did a great job of controlling her emotions over the past week, but she wasn't sure how. She lost her best friend and her husband. Charles died in the ambulance and the doctors were able to stabilize Lisa but she just could not hold on, she died a few days later. Sheila and Corey planned a double funeral with the help of Mama Lena, Mr. and Mrs. Holcomb, Corey's parents, the Martins and Lisa's parents.

"This has been the longest week of my life, said Sheila as she stared in the bathroom mirror. She and Malia stayed with Mona for a few days after everything happened. Sheila hired a cleaning crew to clean and sanitize the house. Once the house was clean, she knew she and Malia needed to return home and resume her life. Charles's death was devastating for two of them.

She and Malia moved back home a few days ago. Elise and Mona thought it was too soon but she told them it was the home she and Charles built for their family and their life. No one could make her leave.

As he put her earrings on, she felt satisfied with the black dress and pill box hat and veil she wore. She heard a knock at the door. "Come in, I'm dressed, she said aloud. Even with all the uncertainty within her and knowing Charles's extra relationships she still loved him. She never expected him to be taken from her life in this manner.

"Sheila, I want you to know that we are so sorry for the awful things our son has did. As a man, a married man of sixty years I know times get hard, relationships get tested, but you never bring anything home to harm or disrespect the home you've built. Mr. Holcomb told her.

"Dad, thank you for those words, but you do not have to apologize for Charles' actions, he did that himself. We all make mistakes and we are not perfect. I can't say what would have happened to our marriage if he were still alive, she said feeling her eyes welling up with tears. "But I can tell you this, I loved Charles and I believe he was sorry for what he had done. I forgave him. I'm not the only one hurting today. You and Mom lost your only son, and my precious daughter has lost her father. Corey lost his wife and our best friend. Many may not understand this but two other people died that day, an old friend, Calvin Hobbes who just wanted to be loved and the person he became being Karl, she said more to herself than her father in law.

She hugged and kissed her father in law to assure him she was doing okay. He left her to finish dressing and headed downstairs to check on his wife. Sheila turned back to the mirror to give her attire one last look. Opening a tube of bright red lipstick, she instantly thought of Karl.

Sheila had a private memorial for him. Since he had no family or friends, authorities cremated him and released his remains to her. She decided to pour his ashes into a stream that flowed through Rock Creek Park. She remembered Lisa telling her that Calvin once told her that he often went to the park when he needed a break when they were in college. Sheila had forgiven him and she wanted to give him a proper burial.

Sheila snapped back to reality and headed out the door and down the hall. She stopped at Malia's bedroom and looked in the doorway. She saw her daughter sitting on her bed holding a white teddy bear. Charles gave her that bear on Valentine's Day when she was five years old. Malia, honey the car is here, you about ready to go? Sheila asked quietly.

Turning to see her mother standing there, Yes, I'm ready, she replied still sitting there solemnly.

Shelia walked into her daughter's room and sat down on the bed next to her.

Lia, I know this is the hardest thing you will probably ever deal with in your life. I know, I've been there too. Somehow, I made it through my Daddy's funeral and each day after that. He loved you with everything in him. Do you know that?" Sheila asked her daughter.

Yes ma'am, she whispered.

I will not lie, today will be difficult. The days to come will sometimes feel like the worse pain you ever felt but trust me honey it will get better. When you feel hurt and pain or just miss them, talk to your Daddy and Auntie they are listening. Today we're just putting the bodies God gave them in the ground, not their spirits. Your Dad and Lisa are here, right here in this very room watching over us, never forget that okay? Sheila told her.

I won't Mommy, I wont, replied Malia.

Sheila and Malia sat sobbing and holding hands tightly. Mother and daughter shed a few more tears, hugged each other tightly.

Well Liaboo, it is time for us to go, are you ready? asked Sheila.

Yes, maam Im ready. No matter what Mom we will always have each other, I love you.

I love you too baby! replied Sheila. Sheila and Malia walked down the stairs holding each others hands knowing the family that waited for them at the bottom of the stairs was all they needed to make it.

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

Epilogue

 

Three years later

 

"Malia, get your purse and come on we are going to be late if we don't leave now! yelled Sheila.

"Coming Mom, I need to turn off the curling iron! replied Malia.

"Curling iron, Carlos just did her hair last night. What is she doing? Sheila said to herself. Sheila watched as Malia came down the stairs. Her eyes welled up with tears as she realized the magnitude of this day. Two years ago, today she and Malia were heading to church to say a final farewell to Charles and Lisa. Sheila worried that losing her father and Lisa would send Malia down a very wrong road. She vowed that day to make sure her baby was okay, but she didn't have to. Malia told her she made a promise to herself, her father, and her Aunt Lisa that she would put her nose in the books and make them proud and she did just that.

Today, Malia is graduating from high school. She was accepted to Howard University on a full academic scholarship and planned to major in psychology. She plans to specialize in the mental health of teenagers and college students. She said that if Calvin I mean Karl had someone else to talk to while he was in college maybe he would not have felt so alone.

Sheila was proud of the compassion her daughter felt regarding the man that killed her father. She used it to motivate her own lifes direction. The whole family is here for her graduation, she would know that already if she would get downstairs.

At that moment Malia stepped out. How do I look? asked Malia twirling around. "You look beautiful, my dear absolutely breathtaking. You will be the most beautiful graduate on that field today! Now can we leave please go? said Sheila smiling.

"Yes ma'am, replied Malia as she opened the front door.

"Surprise Lia! screamed her family.

Malia's family and friends filled the front lawn with balloons, streamers, and noise makers. Lined behind them were six white limousines ready and waiting to escort the graduate and her family to the school.

"Mom what did you do? screamed Malia.

"I didn't do anything, thank your grandparents! laughed Sheila.

Malia ran down the stairs to hug her grandparents and squeal with her friends. She saw Corey and Nina walking up the drive way. She was happy to see Corey and his new wife, who by the way was five months pregnant.

It took Corey sometime to come to terms with his of loss of Lisa, but one day he met Nina and she awakened something in him, she helped him work through the pain and they married ten months ago. Corey said Nina agreed to make their little girl middle name Lisa. Nina is a very special woman.

"Hi you guys! You made it! Nina how are you feeling? Sheila asked after hugging them both.

"Yes, we made it, we wouldn't miss this for the world. That's my god daughter I had to be here! said Corey.

"Yes, I'm armed with ginger ale and crackers but I'm going. Malia lets get going so the graduates can get in place! yelled Sheila.

"Malia you and your friends pile into the first car and get going. Everyone else pick a car and get in! Sheila instructed. Malia ran over to her mother gave her a big hug, also hugging Corey and Nina. She looked at them and smiled.

"You know Daddy and Auntie Lisa are dancing up there right! said Malia.

Sheila and Corey laughed at that since neither of them had any rhythm and both were awful dancers.

"Yes, Liaboo they are doing something up there they would call dancing! said Sheila.

Malia turned to go to her limousine when she noticed James Baker walking up the driveway. "Hi Mr. Baker, thank you for coming! she said before giving him a huge hug.

"I wouldn't miss this for the world, he said handing her a single red rose. Malia turned around and whispered in her mother's ear, "Mom I'm leaving in a few weeks for that summer program at school. I think it's time for you to go out and play! Mr. Baker is fine! she said with a wink before she headed off to the car.

Sheila looked at Corey and Nina, "Did my daughter just give me permission to date? she asked.

Corey and Nina could not hold back their laughter. "See you at the school Sheila! said Corey still laughing as he and Nina headed to one of the limousines.

Shaking her head in amazement, Sheila looked at James as he walked towards her. He had been a great friend over the past two years. Expecting nothing but pure friendship and she would always be grateful for that. Biting her lower lip, He is fine, she thought to herself. Maybe it was time for Sheila to go out and play.

 

The End
